thestockalley Cheap trade pays off. It‚Äôs on you from here.

It's impossible to tell you when to sell when you‚Äôre in the
green because | don‚Äôt know what you want to make. | don‚Äôt
know your goal for that trade, nor do | know how you're
thinking. When | traded, all | did was aim for 20%. If | entered
a cheap trade, | bought a lot of contracts and sold 80% of
them once they were up 20%. If you're trading cautiously and
buying a small amount, then your risk reward ratio becomes
dangerous. If you're going to take a chance, then take it and
go big, so when it pops, you can sell and call it a day. Cheap
trades aren't meant to be held for long. You get in and you
get out. Anything after that is gambling.

go big, so when it pops, you can sell and call it a day. Cheap
trades aren't meant to be held for long. You get in and you
get out. Anything after that is gambling.

thinking. When | traded, all | did was aim for 20%. If | entered

them once they were up 20%. If you're trading cautiously and
buying a small amount, then your risk reward ratio becomes
dangerous. If you're going to take a chance, then take it and
go big, so when it pops, you can sell and call it a day. Cheap
trades aren't meant to be held for long. You get in and you
get out. Anything after that is gambling.
